The corridor on the second floor is even longer, and it feels like the end is almost at Renmin Middle Road. It is also very complicated: corridor-elevator-turn right-corridor-turn right-corridor-turn left-corridor-turn left, like walking through a maze. If you don't have a good memory, you can really get lost. Speechless. 2. Building 8 is currently under renovation. There is dust flying all day long on both sides, the smell is unpleasant, and the sound of electric drills is piercing. You must pass Building 8 every day when entering and exiting. The air is full of dust, and you have to cover your mouth and nose and pass through quickly. Speechless! 3. The free soft drinks in the mini bar of the executive room can only be enjoyed once, and they are not replenished. It is the same whether you stay for a few nights or one night, which is very strange. This is the first time I have encountered it. If you can't afford it, don't waive it. It's too unstructured. "It's enough to mess up the kitchen." Speechless! 4. The network in the guest room is very poor, and you can't access the Internet at all. Changing the router is useless, the turtle speed is always disconnected. I stayed for a few nights and used my own data traffic. Speechless! 5. There is no body lotion and no disposable slippers. The coffee bags were not available one day and they were not replenished. I asked the cleaner why they didn't put 2 bottles of mineral water every day. The answer was that they only put one bottle every day and I could call the front desk if I needed it. Is mineral water expensive? Is this the standard for a five-star hotel? Speechless! 6. Nearly 20 friends drank tea in the lobby bar. A lady who didn't drink tea wanted a glass of boiled water. The waiter said that boiled water would be charged, and the fee was the same as tea. Is this hotel a waste of money? Speechless again! I was really disappointed when I chose Xianheng Hotel when I returned to Shaoxing this time. It is not a little bit worse than Shaoxing Hotel and Shimao Crown Holiday Hotel. I have always been accustomed to giving good reviews, but this time I have to tell the truth based on facts.

msg:Staying in Xianheng is still a good choice during your trip to Shaoxing.
advantage:
1. Convenient transportation and dining: It is at the east entrance of Lu Xun‚Äôs hometown scenic spot. After visiting Lu Xun‚Äôs hometown on the left, cross the road and continue about 300 meters west to reach Shen Garden. Go out and turn right, then turn right on Cangqiao Straight Street for about 15 minutes, and walk to the hometown of Shusheng for about 25 minutes. Taking a taxi to East Lake and Lanting is very convenient, and the furthest trip to Anchang Ancient Town is about 40 yuan. Shaoxing is not big, and the scenic spots are not big either. You can visit all three places in one day. There are 4 restaurants opposite the hotel and on the right hand side. Internet Celebrity Treasure Hunt is at the intersection on the right.
2. Accommodation: Find tranquility amidst the hustle and bustle. Although it is next to a scenic spot, the hotel is very quiet and the rooms are well soundproofed. The waiters are very enthusiastic. 4 bottles of mineral water are provided every day, which is very good.
insufficient:
1. The front desk first gives guests a room with a bad orientation. The feeling is very bad when they first check in.
When I booked a courtyard room for 3 days on Ctrip, the front desk directly gave me a courtyard room facing a wall and a floor. I asked the front desk if there was one facing an interior view, and then I changed the room. Fortunately, we stayed for 4 days and there was no courtyard room on the last day. The front desk proactively suggested changing to a deluxe twin room upstairs for the 4 days, facing the hotel view, which soothed my hurt heart.
2. Breakfast is single. Breakfast is the same dishes and snacks every day, no changes, and no ravioli.
3. As an environmental protection company, we do not provide disposable slippers and toiletries. You need to ask the front desk for support and understanding. However, the shower gel and shampoo are both very, very small bottles, and they are still open. I am worried that the previous customer did not use them up. It's not very hygienic, so it's better to just change it to a wall-mounted squeeze type to make people feel at ease.
